.. index:: pair: typedef; ssh_auth_callback
.. _doxid-libssh_8h_1a3b54d7be70dcc98a107e41e11000a3e1:

.. ref-code-block:: cpp
	:class: doxyrest-title-code-block

	typedef int (*ssh_auth_callback)(
		const char *prompt,
		char *buf,
		size_t len,
		int echo,
		int verify,
		void *userdata
		)

SSH authentication callback.



.. rubric:: Parameters:

.. list-table::
	:widths: 20 80

	*
		- prompt

		- Prompt to be displayed.

	*
		- buf

		- Buffer to save the password. You should null-terminate it.

	*
		- len

		- Length of the buffer.

	*
		- echo

		- Enable or disable the echo of what you type.

	*
		- verify

		- Should the password be verified?

	*
		- userdata

		- Userdata to be passed to the callback function. Useful for GUI applications.



.. rubric:: Returns:

0 on success, < 0 on error.

.. index:: pair: typedef; ssh_poll_callback
.. _doxid-poll_8h_1af2a7809ed930c3f7eb5ab1a086673053:

.. ref-code-block:: cpp
	:class: doxyrest-title-code-block

	typedef int (*ssh_poll_callback)(
		ssh_poll_handle p,
		socket_t fd,
		int revents,
		void *userdata
		)

SSH poll callback.

This callback will be used when an event caught on the socket.



.. rubric:: Parameters:

.. list-table::
	:widths: 20 80

	*
		- p

		- Poll object this callback belongs to.

	*
		- fd

		- The raw socket.

	*
		- revents

		- The current poll events on the socket.

	*
		- userdata

		- Userdata to be passed to the callback function.



.. rubric:: Returns:

0 on success, < 0 if you removed the poll object from its poll context.

.. index:: pair: function; ssh_set_agent_channel
.. _doxid-libssh_8h_1a5cfc7675941d8f82f6c9d08fb020f40e:

.. ref-code-block:: cpp
	:class: doxyrest-title-code-block

	int
	ssh_set_agent_channel(
		ssh_session session,
		ssh_channel channel
	)

sets the SSH agent channel.

The SSH agent channel will be used to authenticate this client using an agent through a channel, from another session. The most likely use is to implement SSH Agent forwarding into a SSH proxy.



.. rubric:: Parameters:

.. list-table::
	:widths: 20 80

	*
		- channel

		- a SSH channel from another session.



.. rubric:: Returns:

SSH_OK in case of success SSH_ERROR in case of an error

.. index:: pair: function; ssh_set_agent_socket
.. _doxid-libssh_8h_1a925a9b6033c304eb6dfb426541f84184:

	:class: doxyrest-title-code-block

	ssh_set_agent_socket(
		ssh_session session,
		:ref:`socket_t<doxid-libssh_8h_1a30353f381f5fccbb956eea1f3a110b6c>` fd
	)

sets the SSH agent socket.

The SSH agent will be used to authenticate this client using the given socket to communicate with the ssh-agent. The caller is responsible for connecting to the socket prior to calling this function.



.. rubric:: Returns:

SSH_OK in case of success SSH_ERROR in case of an error

		const :ref:`ssh_gssapi_creds<doxid-libssh_8h_1affc3a7d505747b757f988aad05163f1e>` creds
	)

Set the forwadable ticket to be given to the server for authentication.

Unlike :ref:`ssh_gssapi_get_creds() <doxid-group__libssh__server_1gab9ca89e12e290a701dced5f7c91bb677>` this is called on the client side of an ssh connection.



.. rubric:: Parameters:

.. list-table::
	:widths: 20 80

	*
		- creds

		- gssapi credentials handle.

.. index:: pair: function; ssh_socket_pollcallback
.. _doxid-socket_8c_1aa57456b012ab138a8665f5014fae4d36:

.. ref-code-block:: cpp
	:class: doxyrest-title-code-block

	int
	ssh_socket_pollcallback(
		struct ssh_poll_handle_struct* p,
		:ref:`socket_t<doxid-libssh_8h_1a30353f381f5fccbb956eea1f3a110b6c>` fd,
		int revents,
		void* v_s
	)

SSH poll callback.

This callback will be used when an event caught on the socket.



.. rubric:: Parameters:

.. list-table::
	:widths: 20 80

	*
		- p

		- Poll object this callback belongs to.

	*
		- fd

		- The raw socket.

	*
		- revents

		- The current poll events on the socket.

	*
		- userdata

		- Userdata to be passed to the callback function, in this case the socket object.



.. rubric:: Returns:

0 on success, < 0 when the poll object has been removed from its poll context.

.. index:: pair: define; discard_const
.. _doxid-priv_8h_1a093400304e754dc7edba84a07ee95bc8:

.. ref-code-block:: cpp
	:class: doxyrest-title-code-block

	#define discard_const(ptr)

This is a hack to fix warnings.

The idea is to use this everywhere that we get the "discarding const" warning by the compiler. That doesn't actually fix the real issue, but marks the place and you can search the code for discard_const.

Please use this macro only when there is no other way to fix the warning. We should use this function in only in a very few places.

Also, please call this via the :ref:`discard_const_p() <doxid-priv_8h_1ab5bfc2dc14f3063fe7345c6259ce85bc>` macro interface, as that makes the return type safe.

.. index:: pair: define; discard_const_p
.. _doxid-priv_8h_1ab5bfc2dc14f3063fe7345c6259ce85bc:

.. ref-code-block:: cpp
	:class: doxyrest-title-code-block

	#define discard_const_p( \
		type, \
		ptr \
	)

Type-safe version of discard_const.
